< Text>
Galaxy Supernova IPA is a single hop India Pale Ale made 4 times per year. 6.5% ABV, 53.9 IBU. Tasting notes: Golden hue; hoppy aroma; crisp, clean with heavy hop flavor. Food pairing: Sandwiches and burgers.

Orange County IPA is an India Pale Ale brewed with fruit. 7.1% ABV, 55.1 IBU. Tasting notes: Golden hue; lighter hoppy flavor with sharp taste. This would be a good starter IPA.

Nuclear Chi Chis is a Session IPA. 4.5% ABV, 41 IBU. Tasting notes: Golden hue; hoppy and citrus aroma; smooth, subtle citrus flavor. Food pairing: Salad, grilled chicken, pork, and seafood.

Voo Doo American Stout ‚Äúis a full-bodied, dark brew that is rich and malty with plenty of roasted barley character. This hearty stout is layered with flavors of roasted barley, chocolate, and coffee coming from the highest quality imported malts. Its creamy long lasting head completed the brew, tempting your taste buds to be spellbound.‚Äù 8.0% ABV, 37.8 IBU. Tasting notes: Dark brown hue; coffee aroma, smooth roasted coffee flavor. Food pairing: Sunday brunch.

Hop Juice Triple IPA ‚Äúuses Premium American2-Row and a touch of light crystal malt to create a solid malt foundation. Five different hop varieties are used in Hop Juice. Now dry hopped with Mosaic for great aroma. Starts out sweet and finishes with the crisp bitterness of a Triple IPA.‚Äù 10.0% ABV, 100 IBU. Tasting notes: Reddish orange hue; Strong hop aroma; strong hop flavor and hint of citrus flavor on the backend. Food pairing: Steak, thick burger, and lamb.

The Herdsman is a barley wine. 11.5% ABV, 84 IBU. Tasting notes: Red hue; Subtle licorice, herbaceous flavor.

Roasted Peanut Stout is a cream stout. 5.7% ABV, 20 IBU. Tasting notes: Dark brown hue; subtle peanut flavor on the backend with a bite; imagine cola with peanut butter. Food pairing: Chocolaty dessert like a brownie sundae.

Tasting Room Anniversary Ale is a ‚ÄúWest Coast Style IPA with pungent Australian hop flavors. Brewed with premium pilsner malt and hopped with Ella, Galaxy, and Simcoe. A light bodied refreshing IPA with aromas of passion fruit, papaya, and mango. Taste is bitter tangerine, grapefruit, and pine. Finishes dry and crisp.‚Äù Tasting notes: Golden hue; Bite on the front end, strong hoppy flavor, dry finish. Food pairing: Pork and chicken.< /Text>

<user_name>Shawn Hadjis<//user_name><Time>1407884584707</Time>< Pictures>

< review>
Left Coast Brewing started making beer in 1995. The company was under a different name and was changed over ten years ago to appeal to a broader market. We won "Best Small Brewery" on the planet at the Wold Beer Cup in 2004 under our previous name.  Originally from New York and moved to California in 1977. There's three generations and seven members of the family involved. We continue to brew award winning beers from our sand to yours. Our pride is in our quality beer and stellar service. Thank you from everyone at Left Coast Brewing. Please enjoy responsibly. Cheers!
Best regards,
Shawn Hadjis< /review>

<Review>We were very disappointed when we arrived at this brewery. We have been to so many breweries and have never been told that children were not allowed. No where was it posted that "No one under 21 allowed". Not only were we embarrassed when we walked in and were told that "no children were allowed" we had our 7 year old with us. But we could hear as we were walking up all the people inside making comments such as "I didn't know this was a family place" and "What would Lagunitas say?". The only other brewery we know of that does not allow anyone under 21 is Iron fist in San Diego, but they clearly state so on their web site. We were very disappointed not only in the customers but especially with the management. To be treated this way when we drove so far just shows the type of people who own and run this business. As well as the type of customers who frequent the place. We will never return here and every micro brewery we go into, we will make sure to tell those customers to avoid the place. I'm sure the beer at this place was not worth the drive anyway.< /Review>< pictures>

<name>Mary Rosenberg< /name><Time>1374602416553</Time><rate>5<//rate>< Text>
My brother was going to get married 6 months ago and the girl is Armenian so they decided that the wedding is going to take place in an Armenian banquet hall . Long story short I was looking for a celebration spot for a while and to be honest with you wasn't expecting much from banquet halls since there are 3 on every street of Glendale. After thorough search I landed here... Monte Cristo in Hollywood (coworker recommended to check it out and so glad I did).
Met with the owner and he gave me a rate which was a little above my budget, but after clear explanation I was told that it includes over 30 (main, appetizer, salads) food, drink, DJ, colorful table cloths, CAKE, fruits, a picture album w/ pictures of that day, video and alcohol. Since there was a wedding that night they actually allowed me to stay and watch. After that I couldn't wait to see our celebration to take place in this gorgeous banquet hall.
Finally the big day arrived and no exaggerations... we had a blast... We got an exceptional service, delicious food, all at a reasonable price. The location was very convenient and everything exceeded our expectations. Food was exquisite (you can tell they are only using fresh, seasonal ingredients inspired by Mediterranean cuisine), spectacular presentation, and first-class service.
I cannot say enough and all of our guests agreed with us about this great restaurant. It was a perfect event and definitely will recommend for all your great occasions.< /Text>

< Text>
We had a great experience here today. Probably one of the nicest Thai restaurants we had eaten at. We have at dined atmany Thai restaurants all over and had some good and bad experiences. This particular restaurant is a pleasant surprise. The food we recieved was great and the service was excellent. We have dined at some great Thai restaurants such as Lotus of Siam which was mention by the late Anthony Bourdain and so we have had some great Thai food both from Southern and  Northern Thailand. What we enjoyed about this restaurant is the service and how helpful they are towards our dining experience.

I do remember the previous Thai restaurant here at this  location and I am so glad that the decor has change. The restaurant is modest and cozy yet has a beautiful interior and a beautiful Thai mural. It has become more inviting and bright instead of the drab decor they once had.

My partner and I were browsing through the menu and decided on some appetizers. We ordered the following.

1. Say Cheese Fries. The were beautifully flavored and not greasy. They were cooked to a beautiful golden brown.

2. Half Moon Puffs. They had a deliscious filling and was cooked perfectly. The curry flavor was wonderful.

Now our main dish is known at the restaurant as Curry Ramen however in Northern Thai Cuisin this is Known as Khao Soi. If you are not familiar with Khao Soi, it is a dish with deep fried egg noodles and regular egg noodles with a curry base broth with coconut milk, which taste similar to massaman curry. Their are many variations that we have tasted and theirs has a wonderful flavor with just a touch of heat. So if you are interested in trying a northern thai dish, I would try the Khao Soi.

We also ordered desert which was a great end to wonderful meal. We had the Fried Banana and Ice Cream. The bananas were wrap and cooked nicely with some drizzled honey and the Ice Cream was flavorful.

The service we had was outstanding and I am glad they remembered us from our last visit.  It has been a while and I was pleasantly surprised they remembered us. As I stated everyone was friendly and helpful and they were also very attentive but not overbearing. They were easy to talk to a well. In fact at the end of our meal we talked about another Northern Thai Dish which is Called Jungle Curry. She said that even though it's not on the menu, she would make it for us. This is what I see as excellent service.

Overal, my partner and I had a wonderful experience and will return soon to try other dishes. The restaurant is beautiful, the service is wonderful, and most of all the food we had was fantastic.< /Text>

Best escape room and Game Master I‚Äôve come across so far. We did operation X13 and out of ~10 I‚Äôve done at different places up and down California, this one was the absolute BEST! Trapped! as a whole  has compelling stories, immersive decorations and staff, a variety of different puzzle types (not just combo locks the whole way through), and creates an experience worth every penny. At the beginning we got some props that came in handy, we found useful items I‚Äôve never come across before, locks and safes I‚Äôd never seen before, and it was awesome. If you‚Äôre looking for one of the best in the area, this is it in my opinion. There is another location in upland too that was very fun. But X13 at the San dimas location was awesome!

<user>114875541051572794024<//user><Name>Ashley Armas</Name><Date>1566554861650<//Date><rating>1< /rating>< review>
I have lived in arcata for about 3 years and my friends and I have always ended our nights out at TJ's thanks to the FORMER friendly staff and reasonable prices. About a year and a half ago I noticed that the clock in TJ's is approximately 10 minutes fast which really isn't a big deal unless you've just bought a drink right before "last call" (which to TJ's is about 1:20-1:30, for reference the neighboring bar Sidelines has last call at 1:45). Anyways, the time on mine(and all my friends' phones) was 1:20 and I had just paid for a drink for my boyfriend and I, when the bartender and security guard made a big deal about us finishing our drinks. I pointed out the fact that their clock is fast intentionally to kick customers out, to which both the bartender AND bouncer agreed and said "I don't care what time it is, I care about you finishing your drinks". At this point I said "I've already paid for my drink so I really don't care, I technically have a few minutes to finish this" at which point the bartender decided the best response to me calling them out was literally fighting me for drink. After a few seconds of the bartender physically grabbing my drink from me, I let go and the bar tender poured the drink all over the bar top. To be honest, i had great satisfaction knowing that the bartender would have to clean up the rest of my drink after he literally wrestled me for it when I had already paid AND tipped him, and legally had AT LEAST 7 minutes left to finished the two sips left of my drink. I really wish TJ's would raise their standards as far as staff goes, when I first moved here TJ's was one of my favorite bars and now I can't even stand being in there because of the new staff and the lower standards they hold to scam incoming college students(not to mention the drug dealing scandals they've had)</review>

< Text>
In reference to parking, I recommend parking on Venice Blvd. because the lot is generally full and there isn't any street parking adjacent to the restaurant.The food was excellent! I ordered a Mediterranean salad and added steak to it. The cashier's recommendation for the vegan cupcake was a great addition for dessert. It wasn't dry like most vegan desserts. The Agua Fresca drink was an absolute winner. My buddy and I were equally tempted to buy an additional glass apiece because it was beyond refreshing. My only criticism is that the busboy came and turned off the outdoor heating lamp, while we were still enjoying our dessert. This was quite rude, considering that we continued to order things and weren't just occupying an empty table. Even I can't give a 5 star, his actions certainly didn't pale the overall experience!</Text>

<Rate>2</Rate>< review>
This tenders greens in particular serves pretty sub par food compared to the one in Marina del Rey. I suppose its the lunch time rush of Culver City, which makes it  a 20-25 minute wait for salad and protein, or maybe its the tiny portions of protein given. I usually order online to spare myself the catastrophe of waiting in their long line, customer service is pretty terrible on the online orders. Place the order, and receive absolutely no confirmation that the order is ready for pickup, when you do call in to check if the order is ready for pickup - you are put on hold for a good 10 minutes. Not a great system guys.

I usually order the steak or albacore tuna on a hot plate. Today's albacore tuna ended up being disgusting, laced with fatty gunk and thick sliced. I needed the salty mashed potatoes to drown out the taste of the not so fresh tuna ACK! I've also ordered the steak plate which often times comes with steak was laced with ungodly amounts of bad fat (the non tasty annoying kind). I'm not sure what it is about this location that serves sub par food, as the Marina del Rey Tender Greens is awesome about serving a fair portion of quality protein.</review>

<text>I generally dislike salad for dinner.  I don't find any joy in approximating the diet of sheep and other pastoral animals.  This places me in the minority in my neighborhood, but the vegan/vegetarian/curious contingent and I can find common ground at Tender Greens.

First of all, Tender Greens contains meat.  Lots of meat.  It's clear when you walk in that we're cooking up both the animals and the field grass they enjoyed in life.  The meat is well prepared and mixed with a great variety of spices and marinades.  They don't give you a ton of salad/meat combos, which is good - the Tender Greens people know better than you what tastes good.  You live in Culver City and are a corporate type, not a chef.  I've had 3 different items  on the menu; all are great.  (I can't recall them exactly.  The main chicken salad, the main asian salad, and a wildcard that I only remember as damn tasty).  Trust them.

Tender Greens closes the deal with a few good choices of beer.  Belgians, a local amber, that kind of thing.  They don't have 10 beers.  They have 3.  Again, they know better than you or I what will taste good with the food.  Don't question it.  Eat your meat salad and get back to your tender offers.  Leave the tender greens to them.< /text><Pics>None< /Pics>< Resp>
